# Tasks Index вҖ” Monorepo Root

This document defines the task lifecycle for **monorepo-level** work вҖ” changes
that touch the shared library layer (`libs/`, `platform/`, `rules/`, `.claude/`,
`tasks/templates/`, `docs/guides/`), monorepo infrastructure (root
`build.gradle`, `settings.gradle`, `.github/workflows/`, `scripts/`,
`TEMPLATE.md`, `CLAUDE.md`), or cross-project workflows where no single
project under `projects/<name>/` is the natural owner.

Project-internal work (anything inside `projects/<name>/apps/`, `specs/`,
`tasks/`, `knowledge/`, `docs/`, `infra/`) continues to use the
**project-level** task lifecycle defined in
`projects/<name>/tasks/INDEX.md`.

---

# Lifecycle

ready вҶ’ in-progress вҶ’ review вҶ’ done

Only tasks in `ready/` may be implemented.

---

# Task Types

- `TASK-MONO-XXX`: monorepo infrastructure (build, CI, scripts, rules library, agents/skills/commands, shared platform docs)

Sequence numbers are global within the `MONO` namespace, starting at `001`.

---

# Move Rules

## (writing a new task) вҶ’ ready
A new monorepo-level task may land directly in `ready/` when:
- the work is scoped to repo-root paths or cross-project concerns
- acceptance criteria are clear
- impact on `projects/<name>/` is enumerated (or explicitly "none")
- if it changes `CLAUDE.md`, `TEMPLATE.md`, `rules/`, or other shared
  contracts, the affected paths are listed in the task

## ready вҶ’ in-progress
Allowed only when implementation starts.

## in-progress вҶ’ review
Allowed only when:
- implementation is complete
- tests are added (where applicable вҖ” some monorepo tasks are pure
  configuration or documentation; the task should declare what counts as
  "verification" up front)
- shared spec / contract / rule updates are completed if required

## review вҶ’ done
Allowed only after review approval.

### Review Rules
- Tasks in `review/` must not be re-implemented directly.
- If review reveals a bug or missing requirement, create a new fix task in `ready/` referencing the original task ID.
- Fix tasks must include the original task ID in their Goal section (e.g. "Fix issue found in TASK-MONO-002").
- Do not modify a task file after it moves to `review/` or `done/`.

### PR Separation Rule (lifecycle вҶ” PR boundary)
Each lifecycle transition lands in its own PR. **Never bundle task spec authoring with implementation in the same PR.**

| Stage | Recommended PR shape |
|---|---|
| `(writing) вҶ’ ready` | **spec PR** вҖ” adds the task file to `ready/` + updates this `INDEX.md` ready list. No implementation code. Multiple specs may share one spec PR; spec + impl must NOT share one. |
| `ready вҶ’ in-progress вҶ’ review` | **impl PR** вҖ” moves the task file through `in-progress/` to `review/` and lands the implementation. Lifecycle moves and impl commits should be separate commits but live in one PR. |
| `review вҶ’ done` | **chore PR** вҖ” moves merged task file(s) from `review/` to `done/` and updates the `INDEX.md` done list with one-line outcome summaries. May batch multiple merged tasks. |

**Close chore must bundle all 3 steps in one commit**:

1. `git mv tasks/review/TASK-XXX.md tasks/done/TASK-XXX.md` (file move).
2. Update the `Status` field inside the moved task file: `review` вҶ’ `done`.
3. Edit `tasks/INDEX.md` вҖ” remove the entry from `## review`, append a 1-line outcome under `## done` (prefix `(impl PR #N лЁём§Җ, commit hash)`).

Skipping step 2 or 3 produces silent drift (e.g. PR #375 only moved the file, leaving `INDEX.md` claiming the task was still in `review/` вҖ” required follow-up PR #376 to reconcile).

**Why**: bundling spec authoring with implementation hides the `ready` lifecycle stage from `main` вҖ” external observers (other developers, AI sessions, audit) read the `ready/` queue to know what's available next. If a task only ever appears in `review/` because spec + impl shipped together, the queue signal is broken.

Established precedents: `chore: file follow-up tasks ... (#110)`, `chore: move merged TASK-MONO-022/023 from review/ to done/ (#114)`, `#118`, `#124`, `#133`, `#137`, `#138`. Same pattern applies to project-level lifecycle (`projects/<name>/tasks/`).

---

# When to Use Root vs Project Tasks

| Scope | Use this lifecycle |
|---|---|
| Changes to `libs/`, `platform/`, `rules/`, `.claude/`, `tasks/templates/`, `docs/guides/`, `CLAUDE.md`, `TEMPLATE.md` | Root `tasks/` |
| Changes to root `build.gradle`, `settings.gradle`, `.github/workflows/`, root `package.json`, `scripts/sync-portfolio.sh` | Root `tasks/` |
| Cross-project changes (PR touches more than one `projects/<name>/` and the change is structural rather than feature-level) | Root `tasks/` |
| Changes inside a single `projects/<name>/` (apps, specs, services, contracts, project-internal docs/infra/scripts) | That project's `projects/<name>/tasks/` |
| Changes that span project tasks + library promotion (e.g. extracting common content from a project into `rules/`) | Pair: a project task that drives the change + a root task that lands the library promotion |

**When in doubt**: if the file paths in the change are purely under
`projects/<name>/`, use the project task lifecycle. If any path lies outside
that, use the root task lifecycle.

---

# Rule

Tasks must not be implemented from `in-progress/`, `review/`, or `done/`.
The single exception is a self-bootstrapping task that creates the root
lifecycle itself вҖ” see `done/TASK-MONO-001-introduce-root-task-lifecycle.md`.

---

ADR-MONO-022 В§D4 **v2(b)** вҖ” ecommerceвҶ”wms inventory reconciliation (**Option B delta**, chosen by AskUserQuestion 2026-06-08 over A wms-as-SoT / C batch / D defer). product-service consumes warehouse-origin wms events (`wms.inventory.received.v1`+`.adjusted.v1`) and applies the **available-quantity delta** (per-`inventoryId` trajectory snapshot) to its sellable stock вҖ” keeping the order-time gate, narrowing dual-bookkeeping drift. Reverse identity (the ADR-flagged cost): wms events carry `skuId`(uuid) not skuCode вҶ’ product-service consumes `wms.master.sku.v1` into a local `skuIdвҶ’skuCode` snapshot, then `skuCodeвҶ’variantId`. **Discovered during impl: `ProductVariant` had no SKU business key (UUID id only) вҶ’ this task adds a `sku` field** (V12 + seed backfill, AskUserQuestion 2026-06-08 over a brittle config-uuid map). **wms untouched** (D6). **Excluded by design**: reservation lifecycle (reserved/released/confirmed вҖ” double-count) + transferred (SKU-invariant). product-service gains its **first inbound consumer infra** (libs/java-messaging dedupe). 2 consumers + 2 snapshot tables + migrations + tests. v2(b) follow-ups named (periodic backstop / seed-gap / multi-warehouse). л¶„м„қ=Opus 4.8 / кө¬нҳ„ к¶ҢмһҘ=Opus.

- `TASK-MONO-075-fix-mono-074-markdown-skip-paths-filter-quirk.md` вҖ” spec PR #424 (squash `5d435660`) + fix impl PR #425 лЁём§Җ (2026-05-13, squash commit `8a81c1a5`). **TASK-MONO-074 axis A (markdown skip) нҡҢк·Җ fix**. м§„лӢЁ: dorny/paths-filter @v3 default `predicate-quantifier: 'some'` мқҙ negation pattern (`!...`) мқ„ "file мқҙ к·ё path glob кіј л§Өм№ӯ м•Ҳ лҗҳл©ҙ л§ҢмЎұ" мңјлЎң нҸүк°Җ вҶ’ markdown-only PR мқҳ `tasks/INDEX.md` к°Җ `!projects/wms-platform/**/*.md` л§ҢмЎұ вҶ’ 5 project flag лӘЁл‘җ true вҶ’ 16/16 job trigger. PR #423 / #424 self-CI л‘җ case мһ¬нҳ„мңјлЎң нҷ•мҰқ. мҳөм…ҳ 1 `predicate-quantifier: 'every'` лҠ” step-level only + multi-positive `libs` filter AND к°•мҡ”лЎң к№Ём§җ (paths-filter README мқёмҡ© кІҖмҰқ) вҶ’ лӢЁлҸ… мӮ¬мҡ© л¶Ҳк°Җ. **мұ„нғқ: мҳөм…ҳ Z (outputs-layer AND composition)** вҖ” мӢ к·ң `code-changed` filter (pure positive, 26к°ң мҪ”л“ң нҷ•мһҘмһҗ/нҢЁн„ҙ enumerate: `.java`/`.kt`/`.ts`/`.tsx`/`.gradle`/`.yaml`/`.yml`/`.json`/`.xml`/`.sql`/`.sh`/`.ps1`/`.properties`/`.css`/`.scss`/`.pem`/`Dockerfile*`/`.env*`/...). `outputs` мқҳ 6 flag (libs/wms/ecommerce/gap/fan/scm) лҘј `original && code-changed` GitHub Actions expression мңјлЎң кі„мӮ°. `workflows` / `contracts` / `observability` лҠ” pure-positive лқј л¬ҙліҖкІҪ. **13 job `if:` мЎ°кұҙ л¬ҙліҖкІҪ** (ліҖкІҪ л©ҙм Ғ мөңмҶҢнҷ”). 5 project flag мқҳ legacy negation л“ӨмқҖ к·ёлҢҖлЎң мң м§Җ (documentation к°Җм№ҳ, AND к°Җ м§„м§ң gate). 3 file / +84 / -25 (ci.yml +84/-23 + INDEX +1/-3 + task file rename + Status). production code 0. **self-CI кІҖмҰқ = 16/16 PASS** (workflows flag вҶ’ full pipeline + observability footprint trigger к№Ңм§Җ вҖ” yaml edit мқҳ нҡҢк·Җ к°Җл“ң нҶөкіј). axis A нҡҢліөмқҳ м§„м •н•ң мӢӨмёЎмқҖ ліё close chore PR (markdown-only) мқҳ self-CI к°Җ кІ°м •м Ғ мҰқкұ°. лҸҷмӢңм—җ TASK-MONO-058 (`!tasks/**`) мқҳ мӢӨнҡЁм„ұлҸ„ к°ҷмқҖ quirk лЎң мҳҒн–Ҙл°ӣмқҖ кІғмқҙ н•Ёк»ҳ м •м •лҗЁ. **мһ”мЎҙ л№„мөңм Ғ**: project flag мқҳ quirk к°Җ outputs AND нӣ„м—җлҸ„ "м–ҙлҠҗ мҪ”л“ң ліҖкІҪмқҙлқјлҸ„ 5 project flag лӢӨ true" л§Ңл“Ұ вҖ” мқҙлҠ” лі„лҸ„ cleanup task (project flag positive лҘј м§„м§ң project л””л үнҶ лҰ¬л§ҢмңјлЎң мўҒнһҲкё°) нӣ„ліҙ. л¶„м„қ=Opus 4.7 / кө¬нҳ„=Opus 4.7.

- `TASK-MONO-074-ci-e2e-skip-and-force-full-flags.md` вҖ” spec PR #421 (squash `6c3a83f5`) + impl PR #422 лЁём§Җ (2026-05-13, squash commit `7deb7bba`). `.github/workflows/ci.yml` path-filter Phase 1 (e2e 3лӢЁкі„ м „лһө вҖ” skip / light / full вҖ” мқҳ мІ« лӢЁкі„). **(A) markdown skip**: `libs` flag + 5 project flag (`wms` / `ecommerce` / `gap` / `fan` / `scm`) м—җ к°Ғк°Ғ `'!**/*.md'` л°Ҹ `'!projects/<n>/**/*.md'` exclusion м¶”к°Җ вҶ’ markdown-only PR (rules/docs/.claude/CLAUDE.md/TEMPLATE.md/spec md лӢЁлҸ… ліҖкІҪ) мқҖ лӘЁл“  flag false вҶ’ e2e + build-and-test лӘЁл‘җ skip. **(B) contracts force-full**: мӢ к·ң `contracts` flag (`projects/*/specs/contracts/**`) + outputs л…ём¶ң. 4 e2e job (`frontend-e2e-smoke`, `e2e-tests`, `fan-platform-e2e`, `scm-platform-e2e`) мқҳ `if:` м—җ `|| needs.changes.outputs.contracts == 'true'` м¶”к°Җ вҶ’ лӢЁмқј project contract ліҖкІҪлҸ„ 5 project + frontend smoke к°•м ң trigger (cross-service consumer breakage gate). мЈјм„қ лё”лЎқ (filter м№ҙнғҲлЎңк·ё + edge-case 2мў… вҖ” markdown-only / contracts-only вҖ” + TASK-MONO-074 reference) лҸҷл°ҳ к°ұмӢ . 3 file / +60 / -27 (ci.yml +55/-26 + INDEX +1/-3 + task file rename). production code 0. **AC 5/5 кө¬нҳ„ н•ӯлӘ© мҷ„лЈҢ + self-CI кІҖмҰқ = 16/16 PASS** (Build & Test + 3 Integration + 3 E2E + Frontend smoke/lint/unit + 4 boot jars + Observability footprint + changes вҖ” full pipeline нҡҢк·Җ к°Җл“ң нҶөкіј, yaml edit мқҳ м•Ҳм „м„ұ кІҖмҰқ мҷ„м„ұ). Deferred мһҗм—° кІҖмҰқ 2мў… (markdown-only PR e2e SKIP / contracts-only PR cross-project force-trigger) = лӢӨмқҢ мһҗм—°л°ңмғқ PR м—җм„ң мӢӨмёЎ мҳҲм •. - `TASK-MONO-050-outbox-publisher-batch-resilience.md` вҖ” PR #349 лЁём§Җ (2026-05-11). `libs/java-messaging` `OutboxPublisher.publishPendingEvents` к°Җ лӢЁмқј row мӢӨнҢЁ мӢң batch break н•ҳлҚҳ invariant gap н•ҙмҶҢ (poison-pill 1кұҙмқҙ batch м „мІҙ мҳҒкө¬ м°ЁлӢЁ к°ҖлҠҘ). `EventSender.send` boolean вҶ’ `SendOutcome` enum (`SUCCESS`/`FAILURE_TRANSIENT`/`FAILURE_PERMANENT`). `OutboxPollingScheduler.sendToKafka` к°Җ `IllegalArgumentException` (resolveTopic кұ°л¶Җ) / `EventSerializationException` вҶ’ PERMANENT, к·ё мҷё Exception вҶ’ TRANSIENT л¶„лҘҳ. PERMANENT л©ҙ `markFailed()` + batch drain кі„мҶҚ (poison-pill кІ©лҰ¬), TRANSIENT л©ҙ PENDING мң м§Җ + return (retry-storm нҡҢн”ј). мӢ к·ң `onPermanentFailure(eventType, aggregateId, e)` hook (default = log-only). `OutboxJpaEntity.markFailed()` no-arg вҖ” `failure_reason` м»¬лҹј лҜёлҸ„мһ… (13 service Flyway migration нҡҢн”ј), мӮ¬мң лҠ” нҳём¶ңл¶Җ `log.error` лЎң мәЎмІҳ + мҡҙмҳҒмһҗк°Җ eventType + aggregateId + publishedAt мңјлЎң лЎңк·ё мғҒкҙҖкҙҖкі„. 13 OutboxPollingScheduler subclass лӘЁл‘җ `sendToKafka` лҜёoverride (resolveTopic + onKafkaSendFailure л§Ң override) вҶ’ API breaking source blast radius = 0. ADR-MONO-004 В§ 4.6 Batch Resilience amendment лҸҷл°ҳ. **CI 15/15 PASS** (Build & Test + 3 Integration jobs + 3 E2E + 4 boot jars + 3 frontend + changes вҖ” Linux runner к°Җ local Windows paging blocker мҡ°нҡҢ). н…ҢмҠӨнҠё: lib unit 45/45 PASS (мӢ к·ң `OutboxPollingSchedulerTest` 4 classification + `OutboxPublisherTest` 4 outcome-dispatch + 1 rewrite + 36 кё°нғҖ), order-service 260/260 PASS, payment-service 98/98 PASS (BE-136 нҡҢк·Җ к°Җл“ң). л¶„м„қ=Opus 4.7 / кө¬нҳ„=Opus.
